# Model Report: N4,4 (Per-Property)

> **ACAS Xu** — N4,4  
> Per-property experiments (property midpoint reference, no rule cap)  
> Generated 2026-03-19

**Model file:** `ACASXU_run2a_4_4_batch_2000.onnx`  
**Properties covered:** prop1, prop2, prop3, prop4 (4 total)  
**Experiment types:** full_rule, per_layer, impl_ablation

## How To Read Counts

- Each `Y/N/T/o` row is one verification query: `(property, ε, true_class, target_label != true_class, rule)`.
- Self-target rows (`target_label == true_class`) are stored as `-` in the CSVs and are excluded from every denominator.
- Denominators in the summary tables count valid queries, not properties, models, or experiment directories.
- For the end-to-end pipeline and a worked example of counts such as `8/40`, see [`COUNTS_AND_PIPELINE.md`](COUNTS_AND_PIPELINE.md).

**Per-model query accounting (the source of denominators such as `8/40`)**

| Property | True class(es) | Valid queries per ε | Formula |
|----------|----------------|---------------------|---------|
| prop1 | 0, 1, 3 | 12 | 3 true classes × 4 non-self targets |
| prop2 | 0, 1, 3 | 12 | 3 true classes × 4 non-self targets |
| prop3 | 3 | 4 | 1 true classes × 4 non-self targets |
| prop4 | 3 | 4 | 1 true classes × 4 non-self targets |
| **Total** | – | **32** | **12 + 12 + 4 + 4** |
